txtGenInfo
REMARKS : -
1.  Even After Taking Printout of the O.S.Registration Form, the modifications can be carried out in an O/S Case from the Login of Deputy / Asst. Commissioner.
2.  In Case of changes in the Adjudication particulars like Release Category of the Item, PP Amount, 
RF Amount, REF Amount etc, the DC / AC may cancel the already carried out Adjudication of an O/S 
and Re-Adjudication of the Case is possible from the Login Menu of DC / AC.
3.  Online Adjudication is not possible for O/S cases with Value of over 5 Lakhs since the value of 
the case is more than the adjudicating powers of DC / AC.

Form55
Form55
Form55
txtGenInfo
REMARKS : -
1.  Even After Taking Printout of the O.S.Registration Form, the modifications can be carried out in an O/S Case from the Login of Deputy / Asst. Commissioner.
2.  In Case of changes in the Adjudication particulars like Release Category of the Item, PP Amount, 
RF Amount, REF Amount etc, the DC / AC may cancel the already carried out Adjudication of an O/S 
and Re-Adjudication of the Case is possible from the Login Menu of DC / AC.
3.  Online Adjudication is not possible for O/S cases with Value of over 5 Lakhs since the value of 
the case is more than the adjudicating powers of DC / AC.
Arial

Arial
txtGenInfo
1.	Before Taking Printout, Check the Correctness of the Passenger's personal details like Name, Address, Passport No.& Date, Date of Birth, Date of Departure etc 
and the inventory of the dutiable goods like description of the goods, proper grouping / categorization of the goods, quantity, 
quantity code, value, free allowance etc.  If any mistake is noticed, then do not use the "Print" option for the corresponding BR / OS / DR document.  Instead use the 
"Modification" option provided in each of the Modules to rectify the mistakes.
2.	The Modification is carried out in two levels viz. Passenger (Master) Level and Item Level.  If the modification is required to be carried in the passenger details, then 
use the 'Master Level'; otherwise if the modification is required in item level like description of goods, quantity, value, free allowance etc., then use the "Item Level" 
Modification.
3.	After Taking Printout, if any mistake is noticed in the BR / OS / DR Document, the same shall be corrected manually on the respective document with the 
concerned officer's initials.  Thereafter, a request shall be made in the 'Register For Corrections' kept in the Server Room for incorporating the corrections in the database.
4.	Date of Departure in all the Modules pertain to the Date of Departure of the Passenger From India so as to determine the Free Allowance admissible to him.
5.	In all the Modules, the Flight Date should be the date on which the Flight actually landed in Chennai and not the date on which the passenger approached the Red 
Channel Counters.
6.           While entering Liquor  Enter the Description of the Item with Brand and For Cigarettes, Enter the Item Description with Brand and No. of Cartons in Brackets.	
7.           In case of query on BR / OS / DR data or generating any report, always use the Server Machine and not the Client Machines.
6.	In case of query on BR / OS / DR data or generating any report, always use the Server Machine and not the Client Machines
Arial
txtMasterInfo
1.Select the Option "Master Creation / Modification " from the Main Menu.
2.Select the required sub-option regarding addition of Airlines Name or Flight No. or Nationality of the Passenger or the Port of Departure / 
Destination.
3.   (a)   In Case of addition of New Airlines Name, enter two parameters viz. the Airlines Code and the Airlines Name and Click the Button "Add the 
Above Airlines Details".  The entered Airlines Details will be added to the database and the same can be checked by clicking the Airlines List 
displayed on the right side.
       (b)   In case of  addition of New Flight No., first select the Required Airlines Name and then enter the Flight No. in 4 digits i.e. the Flight No.123 has 
to be entered as 0123.  Then Click the Button "Add the Above Flight Details".  The entered Flight No. of the concerned Airlines will be added to the 
database and the same can be checked by clicking the Flight No. List displayed on the right side.
       (c)   In the case of addition of new ports or nationality or name of the DC / AC on Duty, enter the same and click the button for addition to the 
database.  Then check the availability of the entered details in the database by scrolling the list on the right side.
Arial
txtDRInfo
1.	Choose the appropriate option in the D/R Module for detaining the goods.  If each of the item under OS has to be packed in a single 
separate package or many of the items Under OS have to be packed in one package, use the option "1 Item in 1 Pkg or Many Items in 1 Pkg".  If an 
item under O/S has to be packed in many packages i.e. if 50 Litres of Liquor has to be packed in 10 packages then choose the option "1 Item in Many 
Packages".  Then enter the proposed number of packages in which the item will be packed.  Thereafter enter the quantity against each of the 
proposed number of packages and then enter the package number and the package type.
2.	While Preparing the Detention Receipts, the 'dashes' or 'underscores' in the 'Type of Detained Pkg' column should be properly filled with 
the corresponding colour and markings of the package.  For example, if a brown colour carton box marked Red Label Whisky is used for detaining 
the goods, then the 'dashes' at the beginning of the type of packages shown in the drop-down menu should be removed and replaced with 	
Brown and the 'dashes' at the end of the type of package should be removed and replaced with Red Label Whisky.
3.	In respect of Detentions of O/S Goods, the Package No. and the Type of Package has to be entered only for goods which are detained and 
the goods which are released to the passenger, the said details should not be filled up and should be left blank.
4.	While detaining many items, the package number and package type entered against them items should be consistent  i.e. If the package 
number is identical, then the identical package type has to be selected from the drop-down menu and the System will not accept even a difference of 	extra space in the entry of type of the packages.
Arial
txtOSInfo
1.	The O.S.Date should be the date on which the Batch / AIU Officers assumed their duties.  Hence in respect of the Offence Cases initiated 
against the passengers arriving by flights after mid-night, the OS Date should be the previous date and the shift should be 'Night' Shift.  The 'Day / 
Night' Shift alongwith the Batch Date is displayed to the Users during the entry of the details of Offence Cases / Baggage Receipts / Detention 
Receipts.  The same may be ensured and in case of any changes, the same may be endorsed in the Register for Modifications kept in the Server 
Room.  For example, for an Offence Case against a passenger arriving by the Flight No.TG-0337 on 03.02.2016 at 0100 hrs,  the OS Date should be 
"02.02.2016"  and not "03.02.2016".
2.	Choose the appropriate option in the O/S Module for registering an Offence Case.  If the O/S goods pertain to a single passenger, use 
option No.1.  If the O/S goods pertain to multiple passengers and individual ownership of the goods could be established among the passengers, 
then use option no.2.  If the O/S Goods pertain to multiple passengers without individual ownership, then use option no.3.
Arial
txtBRInfo
1.	While preparing the B/R, the duty rates displayed against the items shall be ensured and if the displayed duty rates are less, they shall be 
corrected by the ACO so that the correct duty amount is levied for the dutiable goods.  Without the consent of the Baggage Superintendent, the 
displayed duty rates shall not be reduced as it will result in short-collection of duty. 
2.	Choose the appropriate B/R Type for preparing the duty receipts.  The Flight or Baggage B/R has to be used only for the current dutiable 
goods i.e. for the dutiable goods arriving by the flights in the same date and shift of the Batch on Duty.   The SDO B/R has to be used for the dutiable 
goods which arrived by flights prior to the date and shift of the Batch on Duty.  The Gold & Silver B/Rs have to be used only for passengers who are 
importing them as part of their baggage after a minimum stay of 6 months abroad and are in possession of sufficient convertible foreign currency for 
payment of duty.
3.	While preparing the from the OS or DR Details, the System will display only 'Merit' Rate of Duty (i.e. 35%) against all the OS and DR Items.  
If the ACO is satisfied that the passenger is eligible for concessional rate of duty, then he may modify the duty rate by placing the cursor in the 'Rate 
of Duty' Column and modifying the displayed merit rate of duty. The ACO is responsible for the rates of duty displayed against the items in the 
preparation of BR from OS and DR Details.

Text1
